# Task: Debug Query Plan Regression in TiDB Cost-Based Optimizer

## Background
A user reports that after upgrading TiDB, a query that previously used an index scan is now doing a full table scan. The query involves a JOIN between two tables with a WHERE clause on an indexed column.

## Objective
Investigate the cost model in TiDB's query optimizer to identify which component could cause a plan regression where an IndexScan is replaced by a TableFullScan.

## Steps
1. Find the cost model implementation in `pkg/planner/core/` that computes the cost of IndexScan vs TableFullScan
2. Identify the `Stats` struct and how row count estimates feed into the cost calculation
3. Locate where the optimizer compares candidate plans and selects the cheapest
4. Create a file `debug_report.md` in `/workspace/` documenting:
   - The file paths and functions responsible for cost calculation of IndexScan
   - The file paths and functions responsible for cost calculation of TableFullScan
   - The comparison logic that picks the final plan
   - A hypothesis for what parameter change could cause the regression

## Key Reference Files
- `pkg/planner/core/` — optimizer core
- `pkg/planner/cardinality/` — cardinality estimation
- `pkg/statistics/` — statistics framework

## Success Criteria
- debug_report.md exists and contains the relevant file paths
- Report identifies cost model functions for both scan types
- Report includes a plausible regression hypothesis

## What was delivered

**`/workspace/debug_report.md`** — 612-line structured investigation report covering all four required deliverables:

### 1. IndexScan cost — file paths and functions (`§3`)
- **Row size**: `PhysicalIndexScan.getScanRowSize()` → `GetIndexAvgRowSize()` (`cardinality/row_size.go:31`) — index cols only + 19-byte overhead + 1 byte if non-unique; falls back to `8.0 × numCols` when `Pseudo=true`
- **Ver 1 cost** (`plan_cost_ver1.go:425`): `rows × rowSize × 1.5`
- **Ver 2 cost** (`plan_cost_ver2.go:123`): `rows × log₂(rowSize) × 40.70` — no penalty branches
- **Double-read overhead** (`plan_cost_ver2.go:273`): when non-covering, adds `(rows/batchSize × 32) × 6,000,000 + rows × 49.90`

### 2. TableFullScan cost — file paths and functions (`§4`)
- **Row size**: `PhysicalTableScan.getScanRowSize()` → `GetTableAvgRowSize()` (`cardinality/row_size.go:44`) — all projected cols + `RecordRowKeyLen` (8 bytes)
- **Ver 1 cost** (`plan_cost_ver1.go:400`): same linear formula as IndexScan
- **Ver 2 cost** (`plan_cost_ver2.go:140`): `rows × log₂(rowSize) × 40.70` **plus** an optional stale-stats penalty — but the penalty is **gated behind `tidb_opt_prefer_range_scan` (default OFF)**, meaning TableFullScan receives no penalty by default even when stats are pseudo or stale

### 3. Comparison logic (`§5`)
Three sequential gates, all documented with exact line numbers:
1. **Heuristic short-circuit** (`stats.go:565`): unique-point-range paths selected immediately

:= p.SCtx().GetSessionVars()\n        cpuCost := count * sessVars.GetCPUFactor()\n        concurrency := float64(sessVars.ProjectionConcurrency())\n        if concurrency <= 0 {\n                return cpuCost\n        }\n        cpuCost /= concurrency\n        concurrencyCost := (1 + concurrency) * sessVars.GetConcurrencyFactor()\n        return cpuCost + concurrencyCost\n}\n\n// GetPlanCostVer1 calculates the cost of the plan if it has not been calculated yet and returns the cost.\nfunc (p *PhysicalProjection) GetPlanCostVer1(taskType property.TaskType, option *optimizetrace.PlanCostOption) (float64, error) {\n        costFlag := option.CostFlag\n        if p.PlanCostInit && !hasCostFlag(costFlag, costusage.CostFlagRecalculate) {\n                return childCost\n        p.PlanCost += p.GetCost(getCardinality(p, costFlag)) // projection cost\n        p.PlanCostInit = true\n        return p.PlanCost, nil\n}\n\n// GetCost computes cost of index lookup operator itself.\nfunc (p *PhysicalIndexLookUpReader) GetCost(costFlag uint64) (cost float64) {\n        indexPlan, tablePlan := p.indexPlan, p.tablePlan\n        ctx := p.SCtx()\n        sessVars := ctx.GetSessionVars()\n        // Add cost of building table reader executors. Handles are extracted in batch style,\n        // each handle is a range, the CPU cost of building copTasks should be:\n        // (indexRows / batchSize) * batchSize * CPUFactor\n        // Since we don't know the number of copTasks built, ignore these network cost now.\n        indexRows := getCardinality(indexPlan, costFlag)\n        idxCst := indexRows * sessVars.GetCPUFactor()\n        // if the expectCnt is below the paging threshold, using paging API, recalculate idxCst.\n        // paging API reduces the count of index and table rows, however introduces more seek cost.\n        if ctx.GetSessionVars().EnablePaging && p.expectedCnt > 0 && p.expectedCnt <= paging.Threshold {\n                p.Paging = true\n                pagingCst := calcPagingCost(ctx, p.indexPlan, p.expectedCnt)\n                // prevent enlarging the cost because we take paging as a better plan,\n                // if the cost is enlarged, it'll be easier to go another plan.\n                idxCst = math.Min(idxCst, pagingCst)\n        }\n        cost += idxCst\n        // Add cost of worker goroutines in index lookup.\n        numTblWorkers := float64(sessVars.IndexLookupConcurrency())\n        cost += (numTblWorkers + 1) * sessVars.GetConcurrencyFactor()\n        // When building table reader executor for each batch, we would sort the handles. CPU\n        // cost of sort is:\n        // CPUFactor * batchSize * Log2(batchSize) * (indexRows / batchSize)\n        indexLookupSize := float64(sessVars.IndexLookupSize)\n        batchSize := math.Min(indexLookupSize, indexRows)\n        if batchSize > 2 {\n                sortCPUCost := (indexRows * math.Log2(batchSize) * sessVars.GetCPUFactor()) / numTblWorkers\n                cost += sortCPUCost\n        }\n        // Also, we need to sort the retrieved rows if index lookup reader is expected to return\n        // ordered results. Note that row count of these two sorts can be different, if there are\n        // operators above table scan.\n        tableRows := getCardinality(tablePlan, costFlag)\n        selectivity := tableRows / indexRows\n        batchSize = math.Min(indexLookupSize*selectivity, tableRows)\n        if p.keepOrder && batchSize > 2 {\n                sortCPUCost := (tableRows * math.Log2(batchSize) * sessVars.GetCPUFactor()) / numTblWorkers\n                cost += sortCPUCost\n        }\n        return\n}\n\n// GetPlanCostVer1 calculates the cost of the plan if it has not been calculated yet and returns the cost."

\"github.com/pingcap/tidb/pkg/tablecodec\"\n        \"github.com/pingcap/tidb/pkg/util/chunk\"\n)\n\nconst pseudoColSize = 8.0\n\n// GetIndexAvgRowSize computes average row size for a index scan.\nfunc GetIndexAvgRowSize(ctx planctx.PlanContext, coll *statistics.HistColl, cols []*expression.Column, isUnique bool) (size float64) {\n        size = GetAvgRowSize(ctx, coll, cols, true,        if !isUnique {\n                // add the len(\"_\")\n                size++\n        }\n        return\n}\n\n// GetTableAvgRowSize computes average row size for a table scan, exclude the index key-value pairs.\nfunc GetTableAvgRowSize(ctx planctx.PlanContext, coll *statistics.HistColl, cols []*expression.Column, storeType kv.StoreType, handleInCols bool) (size float64) {\n        size = GetAvgRowSize(ctx, coll, cols, false, true)\n        switch storeType {\n        case kv.TiKV:\n                size += tablecodec.RecordRowKeyLen\n                // The `cols` for TiKV always contain the row_id, so prefix row size subtract its length.\n                size -= 8\n        case kv.TiFlash:\n                if !handleInCols {\n                        size += 8 /* row_id length */\n                }\n        }\n        // Avoid errors related to size less than zero\n        size = max(0, size)\n        return\n}\n\n// GetAvgRowSize computes average row size for given columns.\nfunc GetAvgRowSize(ctx planctx.PlanContext, coll *statistics.HistColl, cols []*expression.Column, isEncodedKey bool, isForScan bool) (size float64) {\n        sessionVars := ctx.GetSessionVars()\n        if coll.Pseudo || coll.ColNum() == 0 || coll.RealtimeCount == 0 {\n                size = pseudoColSize * float64(len(cols))\n        } else {\n                for _, col := range cols {\n                        colHist := coll.GetCol(col.UniqueID)\n                        // Normally this would not happen, it is for compatibility with old version stats which\n                        // does not include TotColSize.\n                        if colHist == nil || (!colHist.IsHandle && colHist.TotColSize == 0 && (colHist.NullCount != coll.RealtimeCount)) {\n                                size += pseudoColSize\n                                continue\n                        }\n                        // We differentiate if the column is encoded as key or value, because the resulted size\n                        // is different.\n                        if sessionVars.EnableChunkRPC && !isForScan {\n                                size += AvgColSizeChunkFormat(colHist, coll.RealtimeCount)\n                        } else {\n                                size += AvgColSize(colHist, coll.RealtimeCount, isEncodedKey)\n                        }\n                }\n        }\n        // Avoid errors related to size less than zero\n        size = max(0, size)\n        if sessionVars.EnableChunkRPC && !isForScan {\n                // Add 1/8 byte for each column's nullBitMap byte.\n                return size + float64(len(cols))/8\n        }\n        // Add 1 byte for each column's flag byte. See `encode` for details.\n        return size + float64(len(cols))\n}\n\n// GetAvgRowSizeDataInDiskByRows computes average row size for given columns.\nfunc GetAvgRowSizeDataInDiskByRows(coll *statistics.HistColl, cols []*expression.Column) (size float64) {\n        if coll.Pseudo || coll.ColNum() == 0 || coll.RealtimeCount == 0 {\n                for _, col := range cols {\n                        size += float64(chunk.EstimateTypeWidth(col.GetStaticType()))\n                }\n        } else {\n                for _, col := range cols {\n                        colHist := coll.GetCol(col.UniqueID)\n                        // Normally this would not happen, it is for compatibility with old version stats which\n                        // does not include TotColSize.\n                        if colHist == nil || (!colHist.IsHandle && colHist.TotColSize == 0 && (colHist.NullCount != coll.RealtimeCount)) {\n                                size += float64(chunk.EstimateTypeWidth(col.GetStaticType()))\n                                continue\n                        }\n                        size += AvgColSizeDataInDiskByRows(colHist, coll.RealtimeCount)\n                }\n        }\n        // Add 8 byte for each column's size record. See `DataInDiskByRows` for details.\n        return max(0, size+float64(8*len(cols)))\n}\n\n// AvgColSize is the average column size of the histogram. These sizes are derived from function `encode`\n// and `Datum::ConvertTo`, so we need to update them if those 2 functions are changed.\nfunc AvgColSize(c *statistics.Column, count int64, isKey bool) float64 {\n        if count == 0 {\n                return 0\n        }\n        // Note that, if the handle column is encoded as value, instead of key, i.e,\n        // when the handle column is in a unique index, the real column size may be\n        // smaller than 8 because it is encoded using `EncodeVarint`. Since we don't\n        // know the exact value size now, use 8 as approximation.\n        if c.IsHandle {\n                return 8\n        }\n        histCount := c.TotalRowCount()\n        notNullRatio := 1.0\n        if histCount > 0 {\n                notNullRatio = max(0, 1.0-float64(c.NullCount)/histCount)\n        }\n        switch c.Histogram.Tp.GetType() {\n        case mysql.TypeFloat, mysql.TypeDouble, mysql.TypeDuration, mysql.TypeDate, mysql.TypeDatetime, mysql.TypeTimestamp:\n                return 8 * notNullRatio\n        case mysql.TypeTiny, mysql.TypeShort, mysql.TypeInt24, mysql.TypeLong, mysql.TypeLonglong, mysql.TypeYear, mysql.TypeEnum, mysql.TypeBit, mysql.TypeSet:\n                if isKey {\n                        return 8 * notNullRatio\n                }\n        }\n        // Keep two decimal place.\n        return max(0, math.Round(float64(c.TotColSize)/float64(count)*100)/100)\n}\n\n// AvgColSizeChunkFormat is the average column size of the histogram. These sizes are derived from function `Encode`\n// and `DecodeToChunk`, so we need to update them if those 2 functions are changed.\nfunc AvgColSizeChunkFormat(c *statistics.Column, count int64) float64 {\n        if count == 0 {\n                return 0\n        }\n        fixedLen := chunk.GetFixedLen(c.Histogram.Tp)\n        if fixedLen >= 0 {\n                return float64(fixedLen)\n        }\n        // Keep two decimal place.\n        // Add 8 bytes for unfixed-len type's offsets.\n        // Minus Log2(avgSize) for unfixed-len type LEN.\n        avgSize := float64(c.TotColSize) / float64(count)\n        if avgSize < 1 {\n                return max(0, math.Round(avgSize*100)/100) + 8\n        }\n        return max(0, math.Round((avgSize-math.Log2(avgSize))*100)/100) + 8\n}\n\n// AvgColSizeDataInDiskByRows is the average column size of the histogram. These sizes are derived\n// from `chunk.DataInDiskByRows` so we need to update them if those 2 functions are changed.\nfunc AvgColSizeDataInDiskByRows(c *statistics.Column, count int64) float64 {\n        if count == 0 {\n                return 0\n        }\n        histCount := c.TotalRowCount()\n        notNullRatio := 1.0\n        if histCount > 0 {\n                notNullRatio = 1.0 - float64(c.NullCount)/histCount\n        }\n        size := chunk.GetFixedLen(c.Histogram.Tp)\n        if size >= 0 {\n                return float64(size) * notNullRatio\n        }\n        // Keep two decimal place.\n        // Minus Log2(avgSize) for unfixed-len type LEN.\n        avgSize := float64(c.TotColSize) / float64(count)\n        if avgSize < 1 {\n                return max(0, math.Round((avgSize)*100)/100)\n        }\n        return math.Round((avgSize-math.Log2(avgSize))*100) / 100\n}"

Comparison Logic That Picks the Final Plan\n\nPlan selection is a two-stage process: heuristic pruning first, then cost comparison.\n\n### 5.1 Heuristic short-circuit \u2014 `derivePathStatsAndTryHeuristics` (`stats.go:565`)\n\nBefore `skylinePruning` is reached, a **heuristic pre-pass** eliminates all other paths if any\nsingle path qualifies:\n\n1. **Empty range** \u2192 `TableDual` (zero rows, trivially optimal).\n2. **Point-range on unique index / PK with `IsSingleScan`** \u2192 chosen immediately; all other\n   paths discarded (`ds.PossibleAccessPaths = ds.PossibleAccessPaths[:1]`, line 674-675).\n3. **Point-range on unique index without `IsSingleScan`** \u2192 stored in `uniqueIdxsWithDoubleScan`.\n4. **Covering (single-scan) index** \u2192 stored in `singleScanIdxs`; may be promoted over\n   `uniqueIdxsWithDoubleScan` if it covers strictly more access conditions.\n\nIf no heuristic fires, **all** surviving paths reach skyline pruning.\n\n### 5.2 Skyline pruning \u2014 `skylinePruning` / `compareCandidates` (`find_best_task.go:1119, 714`)\n\n```go\n// find_best_task.go:714\nfunc compareCandidates(sctx, prop, lhs, rhs *candidatePath) int {\n    // Dimension 1: accessCondsColMap \u2014 how many table columns are covered by access conds\n    // Dimension 2: IsSingleScan     \u2014 covering index avoids table fetch\n    // Dimension 3: isMatchProp      \u2014 satisfies ORDER BY without extra sort\n    // Dimension 4: globalIndex      \u2014 global partition index preferred\n    //\n    // Fix45132 (CountAfterAccess ratio):\n    //   if lhs.CountAfterAccess / rhs.CountAfterAccess > 1000, treat lhs as dominated\n    //   (prevents keeping a near-full-scan index over a table scan)\n}\n```\n\nPruning result: `result == 1` \u2192 current candidate is dominated (pruned);\n`result == -1` \u2192 existing candidate is dominated (removed); `0` \u2192 neither dominates.\n\n### 5.3 `preferRangeScan` post-filter \u2014 `skylinePruning` (`find_best_task.go:1175`)\n\n```go\n// find_best_task.go:1175\npreferRange := ds.SCtx().GetSessionVars().GetAllowPreferRangeScan() &&\n               (ds.TableStats.HistColl.Pseudo || ds.TableStats.RowCount < 1)\n```\n\nWhen `preferRange == true` **and** there are multiple candidates:\n- Paths with `HasFullRange` (i.e., full-table scan paths) are removed if any range-scan path\n  exists that has `EqCondCount > 0`, `EqOrInCondCount > 0`, or more index filters than table\n  filters.\n\nWhen `preferRange == false` (the default), **TableFullScan survives skyline pruning** and\ncompetes on raw cost.\n\n### 5.4 Cost comparison \u2014 `compareTaskCost` (`find_best_task.go:349`)\n\n```go\nfunc compareTaskCost(curTask, bestTask base.Task, op) (curIsBetter bool, err error) {\n    curCost,  curInvalid,  _ := getTaskPlanCost(curTask,  op)\n    bestCost, bestInvalid, _ := getTaskPlanCost(bestTask, op)\n    if curInvalid  { return false, nil }\n    if bestInvalid { return true,  nil }\n    return curCost < bestCost, nil\n}\n```\n\nFor **IndexLookup** (non-covering index), `getTaskPlanCost` sums `idxCost + tblCost`\n(`find_best_task.go:401`) before comparing with the raw `TableReader` cost.\n\n---\n\n## 6. Worked Numerical Example\n\nScenario: 1 M-row table, `WHERE status = 'active'` (non-unique index on `status`), 5 columns\n(avg 20 bytes each), index covers only `status` (non-covering \u2192 double-read required).\n\n**Assumptions (Ver 2, defaults, no ANALYZE):**\n```\nRealtimeCount   = 10,000  (PseudoRowCount, table never analyzed)\nPseudo          = true\nscanFactor      = 40.70   (TiKVScan)\nIndexLookupSize = 20,000  (batchSize)\nrequestFactor   = 6,000,000\ncpuFactor       = 49.90\ndistConcurrency = 15      (DistSQLScanConcurrency default)\nlookupConcurrency = 4     (IndexLookupConcurrency default)\n```\n\n### IndexScan (CountAfterAccess via pseudo equal-rate)\n```\nCountAfterAccess = RealtimeCount / pseudoEqualRate = 10,000 / 1,000 = 10 rows\n  (but floor at stats.go:233 may raise this if ds.StatsInfo().RowCount > 10)\nindexRowSize     = pseudoColSize(1 col) + 19 = 8 + 19 = 27 bytes\n\nindexScanCost    = 10 \u00d7 log\u2082(27) \u00d7 40.70  = 10 \u00d7 4.75 \u00d7 40.70 \u2248 1,933\n\n// Double-read overhead:\ndoubleReadTasks   = 10 / 20,000 \u00d7 32  = 0.016\ndoubleReadRequest = 0.016 \u00d7 6,000,000 = 96,000\ndoubleReadCPU     = 10 \u00d7 49.90        =    499\ndoubleReadCost    = 96,499\n\n// Net IndexLookup cost (simplified, ignoring net transfer and distConcurrency):\ntotalIndexCost \u2248 indexScanCost + doubleReadCost / lookupConcurrency\n              \u2248 1,933 + 96,499 / 4  \u2248 1,933 + 24,125  \u2248 26,058\n```\n\n### TableFullScan\n```\ntableRowCount = 10,000  (Pseudo \u2192 PseudoRowCount, no further selectivity on scan)\ntableRowSize  = pseudoColSize(5 cols) + RecordRowKeyLen = 40 + 8 = 48 bytes\n\ntableScanCost = 10,000 \u00d7 log\u2082(48) \u00d7 40.70\n              = 10,000 \u00d7 5.58  \u00d7 40.70  \u2248 2,271,060\n\n// No penalty because allowPreferRangeScan == false (default)\n```\n\n\u2192 **Ver 2 picks IndexScan** (26,058 \u226a 2,271,060) in this pseudo scenario because the\ndouble-read overhead is still far below a full 10,000-row scan.\n\n**Now with real (post-ANALYZE) stats, 1M rows, index selectivity = 0.001:**\n```\nCountAfterAccess = 1,000,000 \u00d7 0.001 = 1,000 rows\nindexRowSize (real histogram) \u2248 12 bytes + 19 = 31 bytes\n\nindexScanCost = 1,000 \u00d7 log\u2082(31) \u00d7 40.70 = 1,000 \u00d7 4.95 \u00d7 40.70 \u2248 201,465\n\ndoubleReadTasks   = 1,000 / 20,000 \u00d7 32 = 1.6\ndoubleReadRequest = 1.6 \u00d7 6,000,000 = 9,600,000\ndoubleReadCPU     = 1,000 \u00d7 49.90   =    49,900\ndoubleReadCost    = 9,649,900\n\ntotalIndexCost \u2248 201,465 + 9,649,900 / 4 \u2248 201,465 + 2,412,475 \u2248 2,613,940\n\ntableRowSize (real) \u2248 100 bytes + 8 = 108 bytes\ntableRowCount       = 1,000,000\n\ntableScanCost = 1,000,000 \u00d7 log\u2082(108) \u00d7 40.70\n              = 1,000,000 \u00d7 6.75  \u00d7 40.70 \u2248 274,725,000\n```\n\u2192 **Still IndexScan wins** by a wide margin. A regression requires one of the conditions in\nSection 7 to be present.\n\n---\n\n## 7. Regression Hypotheses \u2014 Ranked by Likelihood\n\n### H1 \u2014 `IsSingleScan` lost: index is no longer covering (Most Likely)\n\n**Root cause:** A schema change (new column added to `SELECT` list, or column removed from\nindex) causes `isSingleScan()` (`find_best_task.go:1985`) to return `false`. The index path\nis now wrapped in `IndexLookUpReader`, adding the double-read penalty.\n\n**Mechanism:**\n```\nBefore change: IsSingleScan = true  \u2192 IndexScan cost \u2248 rows \u00d7 log\u2082(indexRowSize) \u00d7 40.70\nAfter change:  IsSingleScan = false \u2192 IndexLookup cost adds:\n                 (rows / batchSize \u00d7 32) \u00d7 6,000,000 + rows \u00d7 49.90\n```\nFor a table with moderate row counts (tens of thousands), even a few extra double-read batches\ncan tip the balance toward `TableFullScan`.\n\n**Verification:** Check `EXPLAIN FORMAT='verbose'` for `IndexLookUp` vs `IndexReader`.\nConfirm whether the query or table schema changed to include a column not in the index.\n\n---\n\n### H2 \u2014 Stats not analyzed / `Pseudo = true` + `allowPreferRangeScan` off (High Likelihood)\n\n**Root cause:** `HistColl.Pseudo = true` means the floor at `stats.go:233-234` can raise\n`CountAfterAccess` to `StatsInfo().RowCount / SelectionFactor`. With pseudo stats and a range\npredicate (selectivity \u2248 1/3 via `pseudoLessRate`), `CountAfterAccess` may be raised to\n`10000 / 0.8 = 12,500`, while `TableFullScan` uses the same `10,000`. Combined with the\ndouble-read overhead, IndexScan becomes more expensive.\n\n**The penalty that should protect against this is gated by `allowPreferRangeScan` (default\n`OFF`).** With it off, no penalty is added to `TableFullScan` even for pseudo stats.\n\n**Verification:**\n```sql\nSHOW STATS_META WHERE table_name = '<your_table>';  -- check modify_count vs row_count\nSELECT @@tidb_opt_prefer_range_scan;                -- should be 0 (off)\n```\nIf the table was recently bulk-loaded without `ANALYZE`, or stats auto-analyze is lagging, this\nis the primary suspect.\n\n---\n\n### H3 \u2014 Cost model version upgrade from Ver 1 to Ver 2 (High Likelihood for cross-version regression)\n\n**Root cause:** `DefTiDBCostModelVer` changed from `1` to `2` (`tidb_vars.go:1485`).\n\n**Key formula difference:**\n```\nVer 1: cost = rowCount \u00d7 rowSize \u00d7 scanFactor\n             (linear; every extra byte costs proportionally more)\n\nVer 2: cost = rowCount \u00d7 log\u2082(rowSize) \u00d7 scanFactor\n             (logarithmic; extra bytes compress \u2014 large tables disproportionately cheaper)\n```\n\nUnder Ver 2 the scan factor for TiKV is `40.70` vs Ver 1's `1.5`, but the log\u2082 compression\nmeans that a table with `rowSize = 100` costs only `log\u2082(100) \u2248 6.64\u00d7` vs `index rowSize = 27`\ncosting `log\u2082(27) \u2248 4.75\u00d7` \u2014 a **1.4\u00d7 ratio**. Under Ver 1 the ratio is `100/27 \u2248 3.7\u00d7`,\ndramatically favouring the index. If the index row count is not proportionally lower than the\ntable row count, the Ver 2 ratio may be insufficient to compensate for double-read overhead.\n\n**Verification:**\n```sql\nSELECT @@tidb_cost_model_version;\n```\n\n---\n\n### H4 \u2014 `ModifyCount` drift: penalty condition fails to fire (Moderate Likelihood)\n\n**Root cause:** The Ver 2 TableFullScan penalty (`plan_cost_ver2.go:165-196`) requires\n`allowPreferRangeScan == true` as a gate. Even when `ModifyCount > RealtimeCount` (table has\ndrifted significantly since last `ANALYZE`), no penalty is added by default.\n\n**Specific condition where penalty would fire but doesn't:**\n```\nhasHighModifyCount := ModifyCount > RealtimeCount  // true after heavy deletes/inserts\n// But: preferRangeScanCondition = allowPreferRangeScan && hasFullRangeScan\n//      allowPreferRangeScan is OFF by default \u2192 entire penalty block skipped\n```\n\n**Verification:**\n```sql\nSHOW STATS_META WHERE table_name = '<your_table>';\n-- If modify_count \u226b row_count, stats are stale.\n-- Enable: SET tidb_opt_prefer_range_scan = 1;\n-- Then re-check EXPLAIN.\n```\n\n---\n\n### H5 \u2014 Fix45132 CountAfterAccess ratio threshold triggered (Moderate Likelihood)\n\n**Root cause:** Skyline pruning includes a special check\n(`find_best_task.go:714`, Fix45132):\n```go\n// If lhs.CountAfterAccess / rhs.CountAfterAccess > 1000, lhs is dominated.\n```\nIf the index's `CountAfterAccess` is more than 1000\u00d7 the table's post-filter row count, the\nindex candidate is **removed from the candidate set before cost comparison even happens**.\nThis can occur when a table has grown significantly (high `RealtimeCount`) while the index's\npseudo equal-rate selectivity produces a floor value that exceeds the threshold.\n\n**Verification:** Enable `EXPLAIN FORMAT='verbose'` and check the pruning info line:\n`[table_name] remain after pruning paths for ... given Prop{...}`. If only the table path\nremains, Fix45132 may be the culprit. Disable with:\n```sql\nSET @@tidb_opt_fix_control = '45132:OFF';\n```\n\n---\n\n### H6 \u2014 Selectivity underestimate from `pseudoLessRate` / `pseudoBetweenRate` (Lower Likelihood)\n\n**Root cause:** For range predicates (`>`, `<`, `BETWEEN`), pseudo selectivity uses `1/3` or\n`1/40`. If the actual predicate is highly selective (e.g., `date > '2024-01-01'` on a recent\ntable), pseudo stats vastly overestimate `CountAfterAccess`, inflating the index cost.\n\nMeanwhile, `TableFullScan` row count (`ds.StatsInfo().RowCount`) uses the full-table\n`deriveStatsByFilter` result, which may apply `pseudoEqualRate` on other filter columns and\nproduce a lower estimate \u2014 making the table scan look cheaper.\n\n**Verification:** Run `ANALYZE TABLE` and compare `EXPLAIN` output before and after.\n\n---\n\n## 8. Diagnostic Checklist\n\nRun the following in order to isolate the regression cause:\n\n```sql\n-- 1. Check current plan and cost\nEXPLAIN FORMAT='verbose' <your_query>;\n\n-- 2. Check statistics freshness\nSHOW STATS_META WHERE table_name = '<your_table>';\n-- Look for: modify_count >> row_count  \u2192  H2 / H4\n-- Look for: row_count = 0 or 10000    \u2192  Pseudo stats (H2)\n\n-- 3. Check cost model version\nSELECT @@tidb_cost_model_version;\n-- 2 is current default; compare with 1 via:\nSET tidb_cost_model_version = 1;\nEXPLAIN FORMAT='verbose' <your_query>;\n-- If plan changes back to IndexScan \u2192 H3 confirmed\n\n-- 4. Check prefer-range-scan setting\nSELECT @@tidb_opt_prefer_range_scan;\n-- Try enabling it and re-running:\nSET tidb_opt_prefer_range_scan = 1;\nEXPLAIN FORMAT='verbose' <your_query>;\n-- If plan reverts to IndexScan \u2192 H2 / H4 confirmed\n\n-- 5. Force ANALYZE and recheck\nANALYZE TABLE <your_table> INDEX <your_index>;\nEXPLAIN FORMAT='verbose' <your_query>;\n-- If plan reverts to IndexScan \u2192 stale stats root cause confirmed\n\n-- 6. Check Fix45132 skyline ratio\nSET @@tidb_opt_fix_control = '45132:OFF';\nEXPLAIN FORMAT='verbose' <your_query>;\n-- If plan reverts \u2192 H5 confirmed\n\n-- 7. Check IsSingleScan (double-read detection)\nEXPLAIN FORMAT='verbose' <your_query>;\n-- If the plan shows IndexLookUp (not IndexReader), the index is non-covering \u2192 H1\n-- Check whether queried columns are all within the index definition.\n\n-- 8. Force index to confirm cost delta\nSELECT /*+ USE_INDEX(<table>, <index>) */ ... ;\nEXPLAIN ANALYZE /*+ USE_INDEX(<table>, <index>) */ <your_query>;\n-- Compare actual vs estimated rows to find selectivity errors\n```\n\n### Quick-fix options by hypothesis\n\n| Hypothesis | Immediate mitigation | Long-term fix |\n|-----------|---------------------|--------------|\n| H1 \u2013 Non-covering index | `USE_INDEX` hint or add columns to index | Extend index definition to cover queried columns |\n| H2 \u2013 Pseudo/stale stats | `ANALYZE TABLE` | Configure `tidb_auto_analyze_ratio` / scheduled analyze |\n| H3 \u2013 Ver 2 regression | `SET tidb_cost_model_version = 1` | Tune `tikv_scan_factor` via `SET tidb_opt_cost_factor` knobs |\n| H4 \u2013 No penalty firing | `SET tidb_opt_prefer_range_scan = 1` | Keep stats fresh; or add index hint |\n| H5 \u2013 Fix45132 ratio | `SET @@tidb_opt_fix_control = '45132:OFF'` | Investigate actual `CountAfterAccess` accuracy |\n| H6 \u2013 Pseudo selectivity | `ANALYZE TABLE` | Same as H2 |\n\n---\n\n*Report generated from static source analysis of TiDB monorepo at `/workspace`.*\n*Primary source files: `pkg/planner/core/{find_best_task,plan_cost_ver1,plan_cost_ver2,stats,task,optimizer}.go`,*\n*`pkg/planner/cardinality/{row_size,selectivity,pseudo}.go`,*\n*`pkg/statistics/table.go`, `pkg/sessionctx/variable/tidb_vars.go`,*\n*`pkg/planner/util/fixcontrol/get.go`.*\n",
